#include "confdefs.h"
#include 
/* If setvbuf has the reversed format, exit 0. */
int
main ()
{
  /* This call has the arguments reversed.
     A reversed system may check and see that the address of main
     is not _IOLBF, _IONBF, or _IOFBF, and return nonzero.  */
  if (setvbuf(stdout, _IOLBF, (char *) main, BUFSIZ) != 0)
    return(1);
  putc('\r', stdout);
  return(0);			/* Non-reversed systems segv here.  */
}

#include "confdefs.h"

#include 
#include 
#include 
#include 
#ifdef HAVE_POLL_H
#include 
#else
#include 
#endif
int main() {
	struct pollfd myfds;
	int ret;

	/* check for Darwin bug with respect to "devices" */
	myfds.fd = open("/dev/null", 1);	/* O_WRONLY */
	if (myfds.fd < 0)
		myfds.fd = 0;
	myfds.events = POLLIN;
	myfds.revents = 0;

	ret = poll(&myfds, 1, 100);

	if (ret < 0 || (myfds.revents & POLLNVAL)) {
		ret = -1;
	} else {
		int fd = 0;
		if (!isatty(fd)) {
			fd = open("/dev/tty", 2);	/* O_RDWR */
		}

		if (fd >= 0) {
			/* also check with standard input */
			myfds.fd = fd;
			myfds.events = POLLIN;
			myfds.revents = 0;
			ret = poll(&myfds, 1, 100);
		} else {
			ret = -1;
		}
	}
	return(ret < 0);
}
